## Text Elements
Rocket

- Projectile
  - fast
  - physics based
- Explodes ^kk3Xx6Px

Laser / sniper
- charge up
- either:
  - constant stream 
    of  damage
  - Single Fire
- Self-knockback ^XrYwrqpF

Machine Gun
- High R.O.F.
- projectile
- spread ^F9b1cYzn

- Swaps 
  position of 
  two players ^ZBIjUjIO

- Halts players
  and attacks

- Have a clock progress throbber that
  ticks to each hour position ^1ug79Uq5

Gravity Zone
- Creates an area 
  that attracts or 
  detract players 
  and objects ^T8QnCUPT

- Prevents Dodging  ^ucmISih7

  within a certain

- Can be applied to 
  enemies ^r3zgwk54

- removes movement
